          <div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_4 home-blog et_pb_column_6">
           <div class="et_pb_blog_grid_wrapper">
            <div class="et_pb_blog_grid clearfix et_pb_module et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_blog_0" data-columns="">
             <article class="et_pb_post post-10645 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-caregiver-program category-immigrate-to-canada category-in-the-news category-work-permits" id="post-10645">
              <div class="et_pb_image_container">
               <a class="entry-featured-image-url" href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/2018/02/07/caregiver-pr-streams-closing-nov-29-2019/">
                <img alt="Caregiver PR Streams Closing Nov. 29, 2019" height="250" src="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/D-80-528-NOTICE-CLOSED-UNTIL-FURTHER-NOTICE-400x250.jpg" width="400"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <!-- .et_pb_image_container -->
              <h2 class="entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/2018/02/07/caregiver-pr-streams-closing-nov-29-2019/">
                Caregiver PR Streams Closing Nov. 29, 2019
               </a>
              </h2>
              <p class="post-meta">
               by
               <span class="author vcard">
                <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/author/nir-rozenberg/" title="Posts by Nir Rozenberg">
                 Nir Rozenberg
                </a>
               </span>
               |
               <span class="published">
                Feb 7, 2018
               </span>
               |
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/caregiver-program/" rel="category tag">
                Caregiver Program
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/immigrate-to-canada/" rel="category tag">
                Immigrate to Canada
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/in-the-news/" rel="category tag">
                In the News
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/work-permits/" rel="category tag">
                Work Permits
               </a>
               |  0 Comments
              </p>
              This has come to us as a surprise. Immigration, Refugees and Citizenship Canada (IRCC) announced that they will no longer be accepting applications for the Caring for Children Program or the Caring for People with high Medical Needs Program. While the Canadian...
              <a class="more-link" href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/2018/02/07/caregiver-pr-streams-closing-nov-29-2019/">
               read more
              </a>
             </article>
             <!-- .et_pb_post -->

             <article class="et_pb_post post-10617 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-in-the-news category-new-laws category-permanent-residency" id="post-10617">
              <div class="et_pb_image_container">
               <a class="entry-featured-image-url" href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/2017/11/10/age-dependent-now-22-helping-families-stay-together/">
                <img alt="Age of dependent is now “Under 22” – helping more families stay together!" height="250" src="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/12/15056646_l-400x250.jpg" width="400"/>

              <!-- .et_pb_image_container -->
              <h2 class="entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/2017/11/10/age-dependent-now-22-helping-families-stay-together/">
                Age of dependent is now “Under 22” – helping more families stay together!
               </a>
              </h2>
              <p class="post-meta">
               by
               <span class="author vcard">
                <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/author/nir-rozenberg/" title="Posts by Nir Rozenberg">
                 Nir Rozenberg
                </a>
               </span>
               |
               <span class="published">
                Nov 10, 2017
               </span>
               |
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/in-the-news/" rel="category tag">
                In the News
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/new-laws/" rel="category tag">
                New Laws
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/permanent-residency/" rel="category tag">
                Permanent Residency
               </a>
               |  0 Comments
              </p>
              Good news for families!  As of October 24, 2017, the government of Canada has changed the definition of “dependent child” to “under 22 years of age”.  Previously, the rules were changed to limit the age to Under 19.  This was problematic for...
              <a class="more-link" href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/2017/11/10/age-dependent-now-22-helping-families-stay-together/">
               read more
              </a>
             </article>

              <h2 class="entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/2017/07/28/government-canada-make-start-visa-program-permanent-2018/">
                Government of Canada to make Start-Up Visa Program Permanent in 2018
               </a>
              </h2>
              <p class="post-meta">
               by
               <span class="author vcard">
                <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/author/lee-g/" title="Posts by Lee G">
                 Lee G
                </a>
               </span>
               |
               <span class="published">
                Jul 28, 2017
               </span>
               |

               </a>
               ,
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/immigrate-to-canada/" rel="category tag">

               </a>

               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/in-the-news/" rel="category tag">

               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/category/permanent-residency/" rel="category tag">
                Permanent Residency
               </a>
               |  0 Comments
              </p>
              The Start-Up Visa Program, which was launched in April 2013, invites immigrant entrepreneurs to bring their business to Canada. The program allows entrepreneurs to obtain permanent residence for themselves and their family. This pilot program was aimed at attracting...
              <a class="more-link" href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/2017/07/28/government-canada-make-start-visa-program-permanent-2018/">

              <h2 class="entry-title">
               <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/2017/07/26/global-talent-stream-helps-canadian-businesses-grow/">
                Global Talent Stream Helps Canadian Businesses Grow
               </a>
              </h2>
              <p class="post-meta">
               by
               <span class="author vcard">
                <a href="http://www.theimmigrationteam.com/author/lee-g/" title="Posts by Lee G">
                 Lee G
                </a>
               </span>
               |

              The Global Talent Stream allows highly skilled workers in certain occupations to receive a temporary work permit in two weeks or less. This new option was announced just a few weeks ago as a pillar of Canada’s Global Skills Strategy, which aims to help...

    (function() {function addEventListener(element,event,handler) {
 	if(element.addEventListener) {
 		element.addEventListener(event,handler, false);
 	} else if(element.attachEvent){
 		element.attachEvent('on'+event,handler);
 	}
 }function maybePrefixUrlField() {
 	if(this.value.trim() !== '' && this.value.indexOf('http') !== 0) {
 		this.value = "http://" + this.value;
 	}
 }
 
 var urlFields = document.querySelectorAll('.mc4wp-form input[type="url"]');
 if( urlFields && urlFields.length > 0 ) {
 	for( var j=0; j < urlFields.length; j++ ) {
 		addEventListener(urlFields[j],'blur',maybePrefixUrlField);
 	}
 }/* test if browser supports date fields */
 var testInput = document.createElement('input');
 testInput.setAttribute('type', 'date');
 if( testInput.type !== 'date') {
 
 	/* add placeholder & pattern to all date fields */
 	var dateFields = document.querySelectorAll('.mc4wp-form input[type="date"]');
 	for(var i=0; i<dateFields.length; i++) {
 		if(!dateFields[i].placeholder) {
 			dateFields[i].placeholder = 'YYYY-MM-DD';
 		}
 		if(!dateFields[i].pattern) {
 			dateFields[i].pattern = '[0-9]{4}-(0[1-9]|1[012])-(0[1-9]|1[0-9]|2[0-9]|3[01])';
 		}
 	}
 }
 
 })();
